  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c5e49cde-401e-4098-b0ea-4415a68338dc'
      });
    }

<div id="review_1195678612" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1195678612" />
    <a title="Crystal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40103174-crystal"><img alt="Crystal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1423510663p2/40103174.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1195678612?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Crystal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Crystal" href="/user/show/40103174-crystal">Crystal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40103174-crystal?shelf=books-i-will-never-read">books-i-will-never-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1195678612" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15910433716062155134">My rating is one star. Do you wanna know why? It's because this book is abusive, and no one should read these stories much less write them. This book was about Harry Styles, if you didn't know...which you should because it has a picture of Harry Styles in the cover. Harry Styles is in One Direction, and he's nothing like an abusive jerk in this story, quite the opposite.<br/>Harry, or Hunter, is abusive, both physically (hitting, kicking, etc.) and mentally (name calling, belittling, controlling, etc</span>
  <span id="freeText15910433716062155134" style="display:none">My rating is one star. Do you wanna know why? It's because this book is abusive, and no one should read these stories much less write them. This book was about Harry Styles, if you didn't know...which you should because it has a picture of Harry Styles in the cover. Harry Styles is in One Direction, and he's nothing like an abusive jerk in this story, quite the opposite.<br />Harry, or Hunter, is abusive, both physically (hitting, kicking, etc.) and mentally (name calling, belittling, controlling, etc). He hits the girl, Cassandra, many times in the face. That is abuse. He calls her rude names, "bitch," and controls her. That is abuse. Do not romanticize it or dress it up. Abuse is still abuse and abuse is never okay. But nobody seems to care..? Oh, I know why. His behavior is excused because he has a mental condition. Okay, I guess that's quite okay. If I ever get into a relationship and he never seems to keep his hands off of me, I'll stay with him ONLY if he has a mental condition. ((sarcasm))<br />This story is on Wattpad, a website and an app, where young writers come together to create and explore and really encourage their creativity and writing skills. But if you inspect it, you'll see that the dominant genre is fanfiction that teenage girls wrote. Many include Harry Styles and Luke Hemmings. So, I wouldn't feel so proud about bragging to everyone you got published and it was all thanks to Wattpad.(I reported your story anyway and I'm waiting to get a reply from Wattpad.)<br />This is a miniature <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3927354.Anna_Todd" title="Anna Todd" rel="nofollow noopener">Anna Todd</a>. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3927354.Anna_Todd" title="Anna Todd" rel="nofollow noopener">Anna Todd</a> is greedy and inconsiderate. She's not even a real fan seeing as she doesn't support the boys. Since when did fans in a fandom get their own fandom? <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3927354.Anna_Todd" title="Anna Todd" rel="nofollow noopener">Anna Todd</a> thinks unhealthy relationships are entertaining! She describes After "Fifty Shades of Grey, add Harry Styles, minus the red room." After is a porn book. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23654859.After" title="After by Anna Todd" rel="nofollow noopener">After</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22609286.After_We_Fell__The_After_Series___3_" title="After We Fell (The After Series, #3) by Anna Todd" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Fell</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23497311.After_We_Collided" title="After We Collided by Anna Todd" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Collided</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23258096.After_Ever_Happy" title="After Ever Happy by Anna Todd" rel="nofollow noopener">After Ever Happy</a> is abusive and unhealthy. Why is it so popular? I don't exactly know...<br />You're trying to cash in on money. You don't even care about Harry, do you? If you do, why would you publish it, knowing it could hurt him? You guys, with your abusive and unhealthy relationships, sicken me.<br />And then, if it wasn't abusive enough, you add domestic violence and rape. Like, who does that? If you were trying to make it realistic, then you failed.<br />Do you know what could happen? If a young girl, 16-, reads After, 5SOG, and this book, she's gonna grow up thinking that relationships like those are okay. She's gonna think it's okay and full of love, and she's gonna keep coming back to him because "he's sorry" and "he loves her." And who can forget, "I know I can change him"? (Women who read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10818853.Fifty_Shades_of_Grey__Fifty_Shades___1_" title="Fifty Shades of Grey (Fifty Shades, #1) by E.L. James" rel="nofollow noopener">Fifty Shades of Grey</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23654859.After" title="After by Anna Todd" rel="nofollow noopener">After</a> , and other books that contain unhealthy and abusive relationships are more likely to end up with an abusive partner...)<br /> In the end, the girl ends up with "Hunter." Falling in love with your abuser? Oh, okay, yeah, totally realistic. ((sarcasm again))<br />I would rate this zero stars if I could. I hope you realize what you have done and how disgusting this is. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15910433716062155134" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3006430386" />
    <a title="Patty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3808220-patty"><img alt="Patty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420122767p2/3808220.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3006430386?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty" href="/user/show/3808220-patty">Patty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/45013635-psycho-sitter">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3006430386" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15484669909757177056">Sometimes I like to delve into a good thriller. This was recommended to me, and I have to say, it had me from the first chapter. I was on the edge of my seat! Cassandra is left home with her younger brother, waiting for the sitter that will stay with them while their parents are in Australia. Who shows up? A sitter that they did not expect. Hunter takes these two and from there you will be entranced. Should you like Hunter? Is he crazy? Will these two survive? It has a very interesting plot, tha</span>
  <span id="freeText15484669909757177056" style="display:none">Sometimes I like to delve into a good thriller. This was recommended to me, and I have to say, it had me from the first chapter. I was on the edge of my seat! Cassandra is left home with her younger brother, waiting for the sitter that will stay with them while their parents are in Australia. Who shows up? A sitter that they did not expect. Hunter takes these two and from there you will be entranced. Should you like Hunter? Is he crazy? Will these two survive? It has a very interesting plot, that will keep you guessing, all the way to the very end. There are unusual twists and turns, keeping you listening. I loved the complexity of the characters. Cassie is young, but is very intelligent. Her brother is resilient and Hunter had me wondering if I should love him or hate him! I love this kind of story, making me think and kept surprising me.<br /><br />Narrated by Layla Smith, she had an insight to the story, bringing not only accents, but inflections that fit the each character. I found that she enhanced the suspense and really brought the story to life.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15484669909757177056" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1213355386" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eke" href="/user/show/24298732-eke">Eke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24785184-psycho-sitter">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24298732-eke?shelf=read-own">read-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24298732-eke?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1213355386" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8435793222226301084">2.75 stars.<br/><br/>The story itself was interesting but I guess now I have read a lot of things like Psycho Sitter on Wattpad but it wasn't quite as satisfying as, for example, Baby Doll or Psychotic were for me. So, the only thing I probably liked was the idea of this book.<br/><br/>I was really irritated by the spelling errors and I felt like I was reading an ARC or something even less because well, there were quite a few issues with the editing of this story. I didn't feel as if it was in the hands of an edito</span>
  <span id="freeText8435793222226301084" style="display:none">2.75 stars.<br /><br />The story itself was interesting but I guess now I have read a lot of things like Psycho Sitter on Wattpad but it wasn't quite as satisfying as, for example, Baby Doll or Psychotic were for me. So, the only thing I probably liked was the idea of this book.<br /><br />I was really irritated by the spelling errors and I felt like I was reading an ARC or something even less because well, there were quite a few issues with the editing of this story. I didn't feel as if it was in the hands of an editor at all nor I found any note of there being an editor. I get it though, the author is young - younger than I am - and I know the pain of writing and editing at the same time but at least she should've gone through the story very carefully before publishing it. <br /><br />Also a lot of the backstories, like Lily's, were touched so briefly that it left a lot of questions hanging for me. I would've also liked to learn more about Hunter as well as Zach. It was just that the events happened too quickly in a row and I feel like there should've been more base to it, like Cassandra's parents being at home before leaving and a bit of her school life. <br /><br />I feel like I'm being overly criticizing so I will stop because I don't mean any harm by writing this brief review. If Alex is reading this and feels offended, I'm sorry and I hope you understand. :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="8435793222226301084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<li class='cover' id='bookCover_43884998'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/43884998-what-happens-in-paradise"><img alt="What Happens in Paradise (Paradise, #2)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1569891907l/43884998._SX98_.jpg" />

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XGyP+T2X4PRKjbhxw2ZVFdGvgi4eu0qhvW5IuEfvFJfLTKfRrlmha7XWcdpiMJHIfBGeTG77hUjLzlZcG8+3CQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OLnAAWyqVF6Q5Rgrac2U6Y08Ggxj+EPszLCxafGUTw+vmegp/2QVwW++0YDIm1A0IIIGbhO4jAW6EK+NrbTskQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
